Supported devices

The following list of devices are supported for use with Google Play. For help finding your device, select the first letter of your device manufacturer's name or search for your device.

  • PC: Ctrl + F
  • Mac: Command + F.

To find your model number on your Android device, go to your device's main Settings menu > About Phone or About tablet > Model Number.

Devices are listed in the following format - Marketing Name (Build.os.DEVICE/Build.os.MODEL).

If you're having problems downloading apps on Google Play (play.google.com) or don't have the Google Play Store app, your device may not be supported. If your device isn't listed, your device may have been recently released or isn't listed for other reasons.

If you need more information on whether your device can use Google Play, contact your device manufacturer for support.

Updated: 9/18/2014.
